Hainan Sugar Representatives Make Another Appeal - Second Petition 160

Since the Qiongzhou and Jiujiang Customs detained Hainan native sugar, public sentiment has been greatly angered. Merchants and farmers in various counties have gathered to question the customs officer of Qiongzhou Customs. The local government, in view of this, has on the one hand advised the farmers to wait quietly for handling, and on the other hand responded to the request of the Haikou Chamber of Commerce by sending representatives to attend and try to maintain the situation, and sent representative Xing Juefei to Beijing to petition. The previous report has been repeatedly reported. Here is an excerpt of the representative's second petition to the Executive Yuan: "Presenting a petition to request that the Ministries of Finance and Industry be ordered to resolve the Hainan sugar case as soon as possible to comfort public opinion and relieve the suffering. The native sugar from Qiongya has been coming north without incident. However, since Zhou Li came to Qiongzhou this year to serve as the Customs Officer, he has detained the native sugar out of order, falsely claiming that foreign sugar is mixed in, treating it the same as deer and horses, confiscating and punishing it arbitrarily, doing so once and again, without any physical evidence or legal basis. Its impact on the market and destruction of the rural areas is unprecedented. As a result, more than 100,000 merchants and farmers who produce and sell sugar have been plunged into deep water and fire. All the facts of the matter have been submitted to your review. We have been informed that the Ministries of Finance and Industry have been instructed to jointly investigate and handle the matter. However, a month has passed, and the Ministries of Finance and Industry have not yet seen any solution or guarantee order, causing merchants and farmers to suffer injustice and hardship, and to live day by day without food or clothing. How can they survive this severe winter? The people come from the people and have witnessed the misery and uproar of the people, which cannot be postponed. Fortunately, the authorities in Qiongya have repeatedly comforted them, waiting quietly for the central government to resolve the matter and ensure the safety of our merchants and farmers. Now, the delay in resolving the matter is causing disappointment among the people. The people look back at their hometown, and the interests are deeply felt. Therefore, we do not hesitate to express our views and plead for the people, not avoiding punishment. We humbly beg the President to have mercy on the merchants and farmers, and immediately order the convening of the Ministries of Finance and Industry, sending personnel to the Yuan to jointly discuss a proper protection method, redress all wrongful cases to relieve the difficulties of the merchants and relieve the suffering of the people. Not only will the people alone remember the great virtue, but also more than 100,000 farmers and merchants in Qiongya will eternally remember the great kindness of recovery. We have exhausted our words and are eagerly awaiting orders."

Wusong Telephone Malfunction: Municipal Office Sends Letter Requesting Improvement 161

The telephone service in Wusong District was previously operated by the private Songyang Telephone Company before the war. However, after the January 28th Shanghai Incident, the entire company was destroyed, making it impossible to recover. It was then taken over by the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications. Now that the market has returned to normal, the number of telephone subscribers is increasing daily. However, the telephones are of poor quality and communication is slow, causing complaints from users. When trying to connect to Shanghai, due to limited lines, users must wait a long time, sometimes even an hour without getting through. At times, the sound is too weak to understand. Tang Chengzong, a Wusong Municipal Committee member, believes that the installation of telephones is not only for quick communication of information but also related to social security. If they are ineffective when needed, the impact would be significant. Yesterday, he sent a letter to the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, requesting that five pairs of Songhu telephone lines be added and that all old and damaged telephones be replaced within the shortest possible time, in order to ensure smooth communication and develop the market.

Family Industrial Cooperative: Pioneering Children's Dental Clinic; Three Trainees Admitted Yesterday, One Alternate 162

The Family Industrial Cooperative, manufacturer of the nationally renowned Invincible brand toothpaste and tooth powder, recently noted the lack of attention paid to children's dental health in the country, which directly affects their physical development. To draw the attention of the general public, they have specially invited Dr. Su Jielang, Director of the Dental Department of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau, to organize a relatively large-scale children's dental clinic at the Invincible brand distribution center on Nanjing Road. Since its inception, progress has been made, and the necessary materials and machinery have been manufactured by the cooperative based on modern, world-class dental equipment. Most of the equipment has now been installed. Yesterday was the day for the trainee entrance examination. All applicants arrived at the cooperative on time to take the examination, which was supervised by Dr. Gu Hailing, a dental doctor who studied in Germany, with the assistance of Doctors Tang Jiazhen and Tan Xingzhong, who examined the physical condition of each candidate. As a result, Sheng Zhiqing, Zou Fengying, and He Wenyu were admitted, and Ye Yunying was selected as an alternate. It is reported that the clinic will open in early next month, with exceptionally low fees.

Two Shops on Yuyuan Road, West Shanghai, Burglarized Simultaneously; Tobacco and Paper Shop and Restaurant Suffer Significant Losses; Employee's Wages Also Stolen 163

At 1485 Yuyuan Road in West Shanghai, a double-fronted building houses the He Xing tobacco, paper, and sundry goods shop operated by Cao Yongming on the west side, and a small restaurant operated by Tang Hanru on the east side. They have been in business for many years, with reasonably good trade, attracting the attention of thieves. At 9:15 pm the night before last, six robbers, carrying three handguns, first went to the restaurant, pretending to have dinner. Then, three robbers entered and closed the front door tightly. They pulled out handguns and threatened the seven people from both shops, placing them under surveillance. Two robbers stood guard, while two others went upstairs and forced their way into the bedroom, ransacking it. As a result, the tobacco and paper shop was robbed of 57 silver dollars, 255 paper dollars, and 457 small coins. The restaurant was robbed of 35 paper dollars, one silver dollar, and a lined spring jacket and trousers, as well as a silk gauze shirt and trousers. When the robbers fled with the stolen goods, they also snatched more than 30 dollars in wages from Zhou Zhongfu, an employee of the tobacco shop. Upon learning of this, Tang Bingxiang, the detective squad leader of the Sixth District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, led detectives Sun Shucheng and Yang Zhongjin, along with police officers, to pursue and apprehend the robbers. However, the robbers had already fled without a trace.

Trial Opens for Appeal in the Shao Wenbin Assassination Case 164

Shao Wenbin, the deceased "King of Flower Gambling," nicknamed "Ma Fu A Liu," originally worked as a Tanhuang singer and later switched to running flower gambling houses. He lived at No. 19 Zhilan Lane, Kazei Road, in the French Concession. Because the French Concession police authorities strictly cracked down on flower gambling, he could not stay there and moved to the Far East Hotel on Xizang Road. Due to deep-seated grudges with others in the flower gambling business, at approximately 8:00 pm on July 28th of this year, he was returning home from dinner at the Far East Hotel when he was suddenly ambushed and shot dead by a gang of enemies in front of No. 210 Huage Nie Road in the French Concession. At the same time, the murderer Li Sigen fled to the intersection of Edward Road and Longmen Road, where he resisted arrest by shooting at the detectives who were pursuing him. He was shot and killed by the detectives. After the incident, on the evening of September 14th, the special operations director of the French Concession Police Department, Jin Jiulin, along with patrol detectives and Chinese and foreign detectives from the Zhabei Police Station of the Public Concession, arrested the murderer Zhang Bingrong, a Ningbo native (31 years old, nicknamed "Little Ningbo," formerly a painter), at No. 68 Hongfu Lane, Xin Zha Road. He was interrogated by the Second Special District Court and sentenced on the 23rd of last month to 15 years of imprisonment for joint murder, as previously reported. It is now learned that Zhang has appealed the original sentence to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The High Court has completed the investigation court hearing. Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 pm, the presiding judge Guo Dezhang, along with assessors Fan and Sun, and Chief Prosecutor Zhao Shibei, specially convened a collegial panel to hear the case. According to the appellant Zhang Bingrong, he completely overturned all the points he had confessed to in the original trial, denying that he had gone to commit murder, and stated that he only knew the details of the matter, which was initiated by four others, who invited the deceased Li Sigen and the fugitives Chen Changgen, Li Landi, and Wang Shilong to go together. Li Landi was invited by Wang. He claimed that he was suffering from a fish-mouth sore, and on the night of the incident, he was sleeping in the Lixing Inn at Chujiaqiao and did not go there at all. He also claimed that he had served four years in prison for a theft case in the British Concession and had not been released for long, so he would not dare to commit murder again. He pleaded that he had been wrongly arrested and requested an investigation and redress. The court verified the confession and announced that it would be adjourned for further investigation. The appellant was returned to custody to await further instructions.

Thieves Arrested, Firearms Confiscated 165

On the night of the 22nd of this month, the home of Wang Yongsheng at No. 212 Baker Road was burgled of clothing and other items worth approximately 30 dollars. The incident was reported to the Zhabei Police Station. During the investigation, Wang suspected that Shao Xingsheng (also known as Yin Yuyao), a Ningbo native with whom he had a past dispute, was heavily involved. Yesterday afternoon at 6:15 pm, Chinese Detective Li Shizhong, Detective Leader Tao Rubi, and Bao Detective Ji Binkui went to investigate Shao's residence in the pavilion room at No. 25 Hongfu Lane, Changsha Road. When the detectives arrived, they saw five people sitting in a circle talking, three on the ground and two on the bed. Suspecting that they were robbers, the detectives drew their guns and ordered the five men not to move. At the same time, they telegraphed the police station for reinforcements. The five men were arrested, and a handgun, 100 bullets, a wooden fake handgun, a leather fake handgun, a children's toy handgun, two fake pearl flowers, a pair of pliers, two pawn tickets were confiscated from the room, including under the bed. They were taken back to the police station. Under questioning, the five men were identified as Hu Amao, Li Bingquan, Shao Xingsheng, Chang Aliang, and Xu Xiaobao, all from Ningbo. After investigation, Lu was found to be unrelated and was released immediately. It was also learned that an accomplice, Wu Chenggang, was hiding at No. 54 Hengqing Lane, Beile Road. Wu possessed four handguns, which were hidden in the ceiling above the electric light and could only be retrieved by removing the electric light. The detectives then went to arrest him, but Wu had already fled upon hearing the news. The detectives removed the large electric light in the room and found a hole in the ceiling, but the handguns were gone, presumably taken by Wu. They then returned to the police station. Yesterday morning, Hu Amao and the other three were taken to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Police Lawyer Wang Yaotang stated the facts of the case and requested a postponement for further investigation. When questioned, the defendants all confessed to robbing the residents of two locations on Baoding Road and Huaji Road. Hu Amao wielded the gun, and Chang Aliang acted as a lookout. Judge Xue Lanru verified the confessions and ordered the defendants to be returned to custody for further questioning at a later date.

Private Flower Gambling Operation Convicted 166

Xie Guangming, the chief detective, and Hang Bingquan, the deputy detective, of the gambling squad of the French Concession Police Department, learned that someone had privately set up a large flower gambling operation in a house at No. 1 Song Deli, Julai Da Road, collecting gambling money day and night, amounting to several thousand dollars. At 0:05 pm on the 18th of this month, they, along with Western detectives and patrol detectives, rushed to search and arrest the suspects. They arrested on the spot Jin Hesheng, the owner of the operation, and employees Liu Shugen, Shen Alai, Hua Amao, and Gu Gengen. They confiscated dozens of flower gambling slips, hundreds of dollars in gambling money, and ledgers, along with seventeen gamblers, including Liu Gansheng, Zhou Baoyuan, Shen Afu, Feng Jun, Yang Rongxi, Mao Fusheng, Pu Heshang, Zhou Jifu, Shi Minggen, Zhu Qingyao, Gao Zhongtang, and Shi Jiasong. They were taken to the police station and transferred to the Second Special District Court for prosecution. The case has been concluded after interrogation. Yesterday morning, Judge Qiu Huanxing presided over the Eighth Criminal Court and ordered the defendants to be brought before the court. Jin Hesheng was sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined 500 dollars. Liu Shugen and Shen Alai were each sentenced to three months of imprisonment and fined 300 dollars. Hua Amao was sentenced to three months of imprisonment and fined 60 dollars. Gu Gengen was sentenced to two months of imprisonment and fined 40 dollars. If the fines were converted into imprisonment, they would be calculated at a rate of three dollars per day. The number of days of pre-trial detention would be deducted from the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment or one day for three dollars of the fine. The twelve gamblers, including Liu Gansheng, were each fined ten dollars, which could be converted into imprisonment at a rate of one dollar per day. The gambling tools and gambling money were confiscated according to the list.

Teenage Girl Disappears Repeatedly; Finally, Her Whereabouts Are Unknown; Shen Jinkui Arrested and Detained for Investigation 167

Xu Cai's daughter, Genda, 19 years old, who lives at No. 15 Kunming Road, is of local ethnicity, somewhat attractive, and unmarried. She works as a female worker at the Shanghai Third Cotton Mill in Yangshupu. At 6:00 pm on September 16th, after finishing work at the mill, she disappeared and did not return. Her mother, Xu Cai, asked people to search everywhere, but there was no news. Xu reported the matter to the police station for assistance in finding her, but without success. On the morning of the 28th of that month, Shen Jinkui, a 22-year-old oiling machine mechanic from Yangzhou in the same workshop, told Xu Jinfeng, Genda's cousin, that Genda was living with him at No. 41 Songpan Lane, Songpan Road. He said that she now wanted to go home and that she would be at Dalianwan Road the next morning, and her mother could come to take her back. Xu Jinfeng was overjoyed and immediately informed her widowed mother, Xu Cai, who arrived at the road on time and waited for a long time, but did not see any trace of Genda. Xu returned disappointed. Thinking that her daughter had been seduced and deflowered by Shen, there was nothing she could do. Unwilling to wash dirty linen in public, she thought that her daughter would return home soon, and she would deal with it then. However, until the 3rd of this month, Genda suddenly returned home. Xu only had this one daughter, so she only reprimanded her slightly. Unexpectedly, at around 9:00 am the next morning, Shen and three friends lingered outside the girl's house before leaving. Two hours later, Genda disappeared again. Xu Cai knew that she had gone to Shen's place and let it go. The morning before yesterday, at 8:00 am, Shen Jinkui brought a pair of the girl's trousers to Xu's house, saying that Genda was not at his place. He said that she had claimed to be returning home for several days, so he was returning her clothes. Xu Cai was shocked because her daughter had not returned home, and was in fact being hidden elsewhere, or there might be an accident. She immediately took Shen to Chinese Detective Huang Fugen and brought him to the Huishan Police Station, ordering him to hand over her daughter. The police chief ordered him to be taken into custody. Yesterday morning, he was transferred to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Police Lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated the facts of the case. Then, Xu Jinfeng, the niece of the plaintiff Xu Cai, testified about what happened. When questioned, the defendant insisted that since his late wife had passed away, he and Genda had fallen in love. On the night of September 16th, Genda came to his house of her own accord, willing to stay with him as his wife. He then asked a matchmaker to negotiate, but the matter of the bride price had not yet been resolved. He claimed that he did not know where Genda was now and had not hidden her. He asked for a judgment. Judge Wu Zehan ordered him to be returned to custody for further verification at a later date.

Workers Injured by Damaged Machinery 168

At the Spuncrete Co. cement factory, owned by Western merchants, at No. 1087, intersection of Dongyouheng Road and Alcock Road, there are fifty or sixty male workers. Yesterday afternoon at 4:50 pm, a part of the machinery in the engine room suddenly broke down, injuring two workers on the spot. Both were taken to the Tongren Hospital for treatment. Zhang Qingsheng's injuries were minor, and he was discharged from the hospital after being examined by a doctor.

Injury inflicted when seeking payment of debts 169

Yang Wenbin, 36 years old, from Haimen, rents a flat at a certain house at the end of Baotong Road, Yanjiajiao, in Zhabei. He is a tea room worker at the East Asia Construction Company at No. 22 Yuanmingyuan Road. Chen Songlin, a rickshaw puller who lives with him, borrowed ten dollars from Yang a month ago, which has not yet been repaid. Yesterday morning at around 7:00 am, Yang needed the money urgently and asked Chen to repay the debt. At that time, Chen was drinking alone. Chen, who was deeply superstitious, became furious, saying that Yang should not ask for money so early in the morning, which led to an argument. Chen then used a knife to stab Yang six or seven times in the head and left hand, causing severe bleeding. Municipal Farmers' Association Presents to the Ministry of Industry: Requesting Order for Paper Merchants to Purchase Marshmallow 171

The Shanghai Municipal Farmers' Association yesterday telegraphed a letter to the Ministry of Industry, stating: "Regarding the request to order paper manufacturing companies to purchase marshmallow and save the livelihood of farmers: Recently, rice, wheat, and cotton have suffered successive years of poor harvests, and prices have fallen. Coincidentally, the paper industry in this city, believing that agricultural production was depressed, sought to remedy agriculture and paper-making raw materials from agricultural produce. They encouraged the planting of marshmallow and issued leaflets, advising farmers to plant it. In the past one or two years, some farmers in this city have planted it, and in the neighboring counties of Chuansha and Nanhui in Jiangsu Province, after promotion, many have sown marshmallow and made considerable profits. Unexpectedly, after the autumn harvest this year, when farmers came to Shanghai to sell their crops, they were suddenly rejected by paper mills. The livelihood of farmers has been greatly affected. When rice, wheat, and cotton were the main agricultural products in the past, even if prices were low, they could still be sold cheaply. Now, they are not even available at low prices. How can farmers make a living? They will inevitably become displaced. Moreover, this autumn's wind and rain have caused disasters, and the coastal areas of Chuannan have suffered greatly. After the disaster, the suffering people have goods that are abandoned on the ground. How can they endure it? The Association believes that this matter concerns the livelihood of farmers and has specially prepared this document to present to your Ministry, requesting that the paper manufacturing companies in Shanghai be ordered to purchase marshmallow, or that the disaster relief association in Chuannan be ordered to allocate funds for storage, in order to relieve the farmers. It is hoped that the request will be approved. This would be a great act of kindness. Respectfully submitted to Chen, Minister of Industry, by the Shanghai Municipal Farmers' Association."

Water Fee Committee Delayed in Organization, Eastern District Neighborhoods Rush to Drill Artesian Wells 172

Since the British-owned Shanghai Waterworks Company in the Public Concession implemented the new water meter system, there has been little dispute regarding water fees in the central district. Because real estate is expensive and rents are high in the central district, the water fees calculated based on rent under the previous 7.5 system are not significantly different. Therefore, there is no conflict between the owners and the water company. However, the eastern district has been affected by the Shanghai War, commerce has declined, and rents are low. Moreover, this area is a residential area for workers. The rent for each house is less than 50% of that in the central district, and a single house often houses as many as seven or eight families. Therefore, water consumption is higher than in any other area. Previously, water fees were calculated using the 7.5 system, but now the fees are charged based on the water meter system, with differences ranging from six or seven times to more than ten times. Often, the rent collected by the owners is not enough to pay the water bill, and the residents are unwilling to bear the additional water fees. The water company is also unwilling to compromise, so water cut-off disputes occur from time to time, and the three parties are at odds, making it impossible to resolve the issue. Owners, believing that this stalemate is not beneficial to the citizens, have asked the Real Estate Association to suggest to the Municipal Council that a Water Fee Mediation Committee be organized, with the Municipal Council, the Waterworks Company, and the Real Estate Association making impartial judgments according to the law. Although the Municipal Council has agreed to establish such a committee, its establishment has been delayed to this day. The Municipal Council believes that after the establishment of this committee, there will be many requests for adjudication of water fee disputes, and to avoid trouble, they are deliberately delaying the process. The Real Estate Association has repeatedly sent people to urge the establishment of the committee, but the Municipal Council has not given a concrete response. In order to protect the safety of tenants and seek a permanent solution, various neighborhoods are planning to drill artesian wells.

Wusong: Municipal Ferry Terminal Nears Completion 173

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Public Works is building a municipal ferry terminal on the eastern Bund of Wusong, which is being contracted by the Shanghai Xinzongji Construction Company. Since construction began several months ago, approximately 80-90% of the project has been completed. Recently, wooden planks have been laid, and the project will soon be completed. Therefore, the opening date of the municipal ferry running between Wusong and Shanghai should not be far off. It is reported that the municipal government, in order to revitalize Wusong and the downtown area, has sent letters to Dada Company and others, consulting them to require all ships sailing to Chongming and Jiangbei Nantong to dock at the Wusong ferry terminal for passengers to embark and disembark, to avoid the dangers of small sampans. Cargo can also be loaded and unloaded at the terminal, which is more convenient. After receiving the letter, Dada Company specially commissioned shipowner Lu Genrong to inspect the new terminal under construction in Wusong the day before yesterday. After the inspection, Shipowner Lu said that although the terminal is strong, it is not large, resulting in a small load capacity. Only ships with a capacity of more than five tons can dock there. For large ships, such as Dada's Dalong and Dalun, the terminal needs to have the capacity to withstand a weight of 20 tons before they can dock.

Each Station Should Be Careful: Use Red and White Route Token Bags to Maintain Traffic Safety: Road Bureau Notifies All Stations 174

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration stated that according to the method for using red and white route token bags at each station, white route token bags should be used for trains that do not have other trains meeting at the advancing station, and red route token bags should be used for trains that must meet other trains at the advancing station. This was previously stipulated and ordered to be followed by the Transportation Department. The purpose of using red route token bags is to allow the train drivers to pay attention in advance before entering the station to prevent traffic accidents. Now that the ferry is operating, all vehicles crossing the river on each route do not have wind brake equipment, so it is not easy to stop trains carrying these vehicles. Therefore, it is even easier for accidents to occur when meeting at the advancing station if precautions are not taken in advance. Fearing that the stations will become lax over time, the Transportation Department has sent a circular to all station masters, stating that they must strictly adhere to the previous orders regarding the use of red and white route token bags and use them carefully to maintain traffic safety. If there is a shortage of these route token bags, they should be requested at any time.

Pudong: Bandits Abound in Bailianjing, Ships Repeatedly Robbed 175

From the mouth of the Bailianjing River in Pudong to Liuli Bridge, factories and houses line the banks and are still relatively bustling. Further into the section of Wuniu, about a mile east of Yanjia Bridge, there are almost no houses on either bank, which has always been desolate. Inland ships only have the sound of oars or ballads at night. Recently, bandits have been driving a boat, anchored there, holding a box cannon and looking like smugglers. When they see a passenger ship passing by, they shout and order it to be inspected, boarding the ship to rob it. On the 31st of last month, the Meng Zhengshan ship of Tai Zhi Bridge in Nanhui was robbed of more than 200 dollars. On the early tide of the 20th of this month, the Zhang Lanmei ship of Jiangjia Road was robbed of more than 170 dollars. The Xiao Amao ship of Chuansha was robbed of two silver dollars and 4,000 copper coins. A single family's ship was robbed of cotton quilts and other items. The Tang Ashui ship of Heqing was robbed of 250 dollars. It is said that when the bandits' boat enters the port, only one person initially rows the boat, no different from an ordinary boat. The remaining bandits walk on the shore until they gather at that location to guard against the investigation of local land and water police and to facilitate escape. It is reported that the shipowners have elected representatives to the Pudong Association of Fellow Villagers, asking the Municipal Public Security Bureau to quickly order the responsible police to arrest the bandits and ensure the safety of travelers.

Tobacco and Candy Colleagues Appeal for Relief from the Guild 176

Due to the harassment of investigations by the tobacco and alcohol tax authorities, more than 30 tobacco and candy businesses in the South Shanghai area and Pudong jointly elected Mi Chuxin, Guo Jingshun, Chen Heting, and other representatives. Yesterday, they sent separate letters to the South Shanghai Office and Chen Liangyu, Chairman of the Guild, appealing for assistance in relief measures. The original letter is recorded below: "Respectfully, recently, counterfeit cigarettes and miscellaneous cigars have re-emerged in the market. Colleagues who are unaware are often fooled, resulting in fines, ranging from hundreds of dollars to tens of dollars. The number of people fined is countless. The colleagues work hard for 14 hours a day to make a small profit to support their families, which is already difficult. This unexpected disaster, although deserved, should be pitied. Now, the commercial decline has led to many unemployed in society. Those who have little savings often set up a small tobacco and candy shop to make a living, because this type of business is simple and convenient. Therefore, the establishment of tobacco and candy shops has increased like bamboo shoots after a rain, becoming increasingly prevalent. However, they do not have sufficient knowledge of tobacco and candy, which has led to this error. Not only are there counterfeit cigarettes, but also harassment from tobacco license taxes. The most important thing at present is the impact of the decline in steel yuan, as well as the competition among businesses, leading to price cuts, even to the point where there is no profit to be made, resulting in losses. If this continues, the colleagues themselves will be in danger. If you ask any colleague, they will shake their heads and frown, expressing their infinite pain. As the 'Little Reporter' said, 'The humble voices of the common people will of course not be heard by the high and mighty ears.' These words are truly painful. To whom can we, the tobacco and candy colleagues, turn to for our hidden pain? If we do not seek help from ourselves, but seek help from others, what is the point? It is believed that the purpose of the establishment of the guild is to maintain and enhance the common interests of the colleagues and to correct the malpractices of the business. Now that the guild has been established for several years, the directors and supervisors are all outstanding members of the industry. They must know the pain of their own bodies, but why have they not been heard to have made any contributions to the colleagues? It is truly regrettable. The articles of association and the industry regulations are also equal to written documents, waste paper. Is it that the things cannot be done, or are they not willing to do them? However, the colleagues hope that they will discuss the methods of maintaining the business from declining, increasing their knowledge of the business to prevent being deceived by fake cigarettes, alleviating the harassment of license taxes, and correcting the competition of price cuts and cheap sales, just like longing for clouds in a severe drought. If they are slow to act, they will be held accountable for the responsibilities entrusted to them by the colleagues. The members witness this situation and are distressed. Therefore, we make these suggestions to the directors, hoping that they will take action to plan and relieve the colleagues from their suffering. We are extremely grateful and pray for success."

Nantong Dasheng Yarn Factory Held Shareholders Meeting in Shanghai Yesterday, Chen Guangfu, Zhao Shuyong, and Others Elected; Jiangsu Provincial Government Appoints Official Shareholder Directors 177

Nantong Dasheng No. 1 Textile Factory convened its 35th shareholders meeting at the Hong Kong Road Bankers Association yesterday at 4 PM. Shareholders present included Hong Lanfan, Wu Yunliang, Cheng Botang, Wu Cheng, and Chen Guangfu, totaling 147 households, representing a share capital of 2,013,250 taels of silver, equivalent to 40,365 shares and 7,235 voting rights. Zhang Xiaoruo was publicly elected as chairman. After formal procedures, the chairman delivered a report, stating briefly that the factory's operational guidelines and reform plans had been reported in detail in the previous session. During this operating period, the country was facing its most severe national crisis. The flames of war raged, and the people suffered greatly, leading to a gradual decline in market prices. Business was sluggish. By the turn of winter and spring, the war in North China had reignited, further hindering sales. At that time, Shanghai alone had an accumulation of over 100,000 bales of yarn and more than 3 million bolts of cloth. After discussions among industry peers, it was decided to suspend work and reduce spinning to provide some relief. However, this did not address the root cause. The price of raw cotton, driven by urgent factory needs, conversely increased, raising costs and leading to greater losses. Japanese factories, with large quantities of finished goods, disregarded costs and dumped goods on our market at reduced prices, putting significant pressure on Chinese factories. Textile businesses in various regions were suspending operations or going bankrupt one after another. Our factory, amidst these turbulent waves, acted prudently and cautiously. We spun and sold yarn and cloth as we produced them, fortunately avoiding stockpiling. In June, while seeking to reorganize operations, we unfortunately experienced a labor strike, which lasted for over a month before it was resolved. There were some inevitable losses at that time, but the factory would not have incurred a loss otherwise. However, considering the subsequent improvement of operations, the savings were substantial. Weighing the gains and losses, it may not have been a misfortune. However, to consolidate the factory's foundation, this session allocated 170,000 yuan from the remaining American cotton surplus from the previous session to the power plant fund. Additionally, over 160,000 yuan was allocated monthly to enhance machinery and buildings. The two items totaled over 330,000 yuan. In reality, there was still a surplus. This can be considered a great fortune. This is the general situation of this session. In addition, to improve cotton cultivation, we specially hired experts this year to promote cultivation in the salt reclamation areas. The autumn harvest was bountiful, and the benefits were already evident. In the future, we plan to continue our efforts, hoping that in three to five years, Jiangbei can produce a large quantity of fine lint raw cotton, achieving self-sufficiency and avoiding reliance on foreigners. The power plant project is also progressing step by step according to the planned schedule. Motors and boilers are being delivered one after another. It is expected that in April or May next year, we can start the machines to supply power for our factory. The above two matters are closely related to the factory's future and must be diligently managed. We hope that the shareholders will provide guidance and instruction. After the chairman's report, discussions began immediately. The resolutions are as follows: (1) In accordance with the Ministry's order, the stock value will be changed from taels to yuan. (Resolution) The company's total share capital is 5,600,000 yuan, divided into 80,000 shares, each share worth 70 yuan. (2) Amendment to Article 24 of Chapter 4 of the company's articles of association. (Resolution) Directors and supervisors shall be elected by the shareholders' meeting from among the shareholders. Anyone with 40 or more shares in the company shall have the right to be elected. (3) When the company issues new shares, in accordance with the Ministry's regulations, a stamp shall be affixed to the shares to simplify procedures. (Resolution) The original proposal was approved. (4) The factory's workers requested a change in the distribution of surplus. (Resolution) Adhering to the principle of not harming the interests of both labor and capital, the matter shall be handled by the board of directors. (5) The company's annual report to the shareholders' meeting proposes to add a property directory. (Resolution) The original proposal was approved. After the discussions, shareholders voted to elect Xia Yucheng, Hong Lanyou, Wu Jichen, Zhou Meiquan, Zhao Shuyong, Li Qiqing, Shen Ranmou, Gao Rufu, and Cheng Botang as directors, and Chen Guangfu, Fang Juchuan, and Yun Jikun as supervisors. In addition to the commercial shares, the factory originally had official shares. In accordance with the regulations, there should be five official shareholder directors and one supervisor. The original letter from the Jiangsu Provincial Government is recorded below: According to the proposal of the chairman at the 609th meeting of the Provincial Government Committee, please appoint Hong Lanyou, Wu Baofeng, Li Yunliang, Cheng Peng, and Wu Cheng as official shareholder directors of Dasheng Yarn Factory, and Chen Guangfu as supervisor. The proposal has been approved. In addition to distributing the order, a corresponding letter is sent to your factory for your information.

China Life Insurance Advancement Association Expands Organization 178

Life insurance in our country, like other industries, is still in its infancy. The intrusion of foreign merchants and the outflow of profits and rights have become undeniable facts. Although several state-run companies have been established recently, most of them hold the principle of "each sweeps the snow from his own doorstep," indifferent to each other, like a heap of loose sand, with no unity. If this continues, what can be imagined? Recently, five Chinese-owned life insurance companies in this city have united to organize the only propaganda agency in China's life insurance industry, named the China Life Insurance Advancement Association. The purpose is nothing more than to instill life insurance knowledge into the Chinese people as much as possible, so that the life insurance business can become common or socialized in our country. The president of the association is Zhang Sixu, the former director of the Intelligence Department when Chen Youren was the foreign minister two years ago. Mr. Zhang is one of the famous reporters in Shanghai, with extremely rich knowledge and experience. According to Mr. Zhang, the life insurance companies supporting the association include Huaan, Taishan, Ning Shao, Sincere, and China. Among the foreign companies that agree and are willing to join the cooperation are American-owned American International Assurance (AIA) and British-owned Four Seas Life Insurance, both of which have general manager offices in Shanghai and have a considerable history. Mr. Zhang also said that about a year ago, he obtained the support of the above three companies and began planning the organization of the Advancement Association. At that time, the prototype was barely formed and the operation was difficult. Although there were not many achievements in the past year, it has now won the sympathy of most companies in the country, and they have eagerly participated. Our mission in the future is to work hard and use various methods, such as advertisements, illustrations, publicity texts, and lectures, to conduct widespread publicity in the country, instill life insurance knowledge as much as possible, and encourage the Chinese people's interest in life insurance, so that the life insurance business in our country can flourish and grow, and reach a perfect state. We should also break the old concepts of the Chinese people, so that everyone recognizes the effectiveness of life insurance and understands the benefits of life insurance. According to the reason for the slow progress of life insurance in our country, there are probably two: first, because most people cannot really understand the principles of life insurance; second, because the ideology of the patriarchal society has been unbreakable for thousands of years in our country, and the concept of the family system is too deep, so they absolutely do not know the joint responsibility. Although this is the case, in recent times, with the eastward spread of European customs, the economic and social situation of our country has been undergoing rapid changes. Life insurance in our country seems to have occupied a considerable position. The future progress is truly unlimited. The emergence of new companies is like bamboo shoots after a rain. Bankers such as Song Hanzhang, Li Ming, and Xu Xinliu have also joined the life insurance industry to cooperate. It is really a good phenomenon.

The poison of flower gambling is worse than floods and ferocious beasts. Special Educational Funds for Zhejiang Province: Guarantee Measures Established丨Implemented in Three Phases丨First, Allocate 90,000 Monthly from Foil Tax Items丨Provincial Government Meeting Decision Imminent for Implementation 195

(Hangzhou Dispatch) Special funds have been designated to guarantee educational expenses for Zhejiang Province. Since provincial schools submitted opinions to the provincial government last year, Chairman Lu and other members of the provincial government have expressed strong support in principle. However, due to the province's severe financial difficulties, it was impossible to designate a large sum of money immediately. Although the matter was recognized as essential, plans were to be made gradually as opportunities arose. In the past month, the Education Department and the Finance Department have been actively working to achieve this goal. After thorough discussions between Directors Zhou and Chen of the two departments, a general framework has reportedly been established. The two departments have jointly drafted measures for the custody and payment of special provincial education funds, which have been submitted to the Provincial Government Committee for review. Implementation will commence upon approval by the provincial government meeting. It is reported that the special fund custody measures stipulate implementation in three phases. The first phase will designate funds from foil tax items, initially allocating only 90,000 yuan per month, totaling 1.08 million yuan per year, starting from November. The second phase will also designate funds from foil tax items, initially allocating 100,000 yuan per month, totaling 1.2 million yuan per year, plus the total amount of tobacco and alcohol surcharges, approximately 200,000 yuan per year, totaling 1.4 million yuan, starting from July of the 23rd year [of the Republic]. The third phase will begin in May of the 24th year [of the Republic] (when the slaughter tax mortgage expires), adding approximately 600,000 yuan annually from the slaughter tax in addition to the aforementioned foil tax and tobacco and alcohol surcharges, bringing the total to 2 million yuan, roughly equivalent to the budgeted amount for education expenses this year (excluding administrative expenses for the Education Department and educational income such as tuition fees). Detailed measures are expected to be announced within three to five days.

Zhejiang Education Department Sets Date for Spring Elementary School Graduation Exams 196

(Hangzhou Dispatch) The Zhejiang Education Department, with the end of the first semester of this year approaching, is urgently preparing for the graduation exams for primary and secondary schools. The official date for the secondary school graduation exam has been set to begin on January 9 of the 23rd year [of the Republic]. It is now learned that the spring graduation exam for elementary schools in various counties and cities has also been scheduled for January 5 of the 23rd year [of the Republic] as the main exam date, with January 8 as the re-examination date. Notices have already been sent to various counties and cities, prohibiting changes without justification. In addition, instructions have been issued that test questions for each subject will be compiled, printed, and distributed by the Education Department, and that the number of graduating students from each elementary school and the number of test booklets needed must be reported within five days of receiving the notice.

China Boy Scout Specialization Training Qualification Standards (2) 197

(17) Laundry: 1. Ability to wash colored cotton, linen, wool, and silk fabrics; 2. Ability to dry-clean rayon and wool fabrics; 3. Ability to starch, iron, and fold clothes; 4. Knowledge of various dyeing materials and methods; 5. Ability to dye a piece of cloth or silk.

(18) Nursing: 1. Knowledge of the layout and cleanliness of a sickroom and temperature regulation; 2. Knowledge of regulating a patient's diet and changing bedding; 3. Ability to measure body temperature, pulse, and respiration; 4. Ability to observe a patient's complexion and record symptoms; 5. Knowledge of various disinfection methods; 6. Knowledge of common sense and attitudes for administering medication and providing care; 7. One week of practical nursing experience with a physician's certificate of qualification.

(19) Astronomy: 1. General knowledge of celestial bodies and their movements; 2. Ability to identify at least six major constellations; 3. Ability to determine north using other constellations besides Polaris; 4. Ability to calculate time at night using stars and the moon; 5. Knowledge of the relationship between the Earth, Sun, and Moon and the basics of tides, eclipses, planets, meteors, and sunspots; 6. Having visited a major observatory and prepared a report.

(20) Aircraft: 1. Knowledge of the principles of flight for airplanes, airships, and balloons; 2. Brief knowledge of the history of airplane development; 3. Knowledge of the internal machinery and external structure of airplanes and airships; 4. Ability to build a model airship or airplane that can fly over 25 meters; 5. Knowledge of aircraft attack defense methods.

(21) Signaling: 1. Ability to send and receive the following two-flag signals in at least two of the following forms: A. Sending and receiving Chinese (Morse code) flag signals at 15 characters per minute, with familiarity with radicals; B. Sending and receiving Western alphabet signals at 35 characters per minute; C. Sending and receiving stroke flag signals at 35 flags per minute; 2. Ability to send and receive the following single-flag signals in at least two of the following forms: A. Sending and receiving Chinese (Morse code) flag signals at 7 characters per minute; B. Sending and receiving Western alphabet signals at 25 characters per minute; C. Sending and receiving stroke flag signals at 25 flags per minute; 3. Ability to send and receive messages using sound (Chinese signals at 8 characters per minute, Western alphabet and stroke flags at 35 per minute); 4. Ability to send and receive messages using light (Chinese signals at 7 characters per minute, Western alphabet and stroke flags at 25 per minute); 5. Familiarity with various set phrases, symbols, and pyrotechnic signals.

(22) Abacus: 1. Familiarity with the meaning of addition, subtraction, multiplication, division, and mnemonic rhymes; 2. Knowledge of the application of various calculations in commerce; 3. Knowledge of the application of fly-back techniques.

(23) Firefighting: 1. Knowledge of the organization of the local fire brigade and how to report a fire; 2. Knowledge of how to enter and exit a burning building; 3. Knowledge of methods for preventing the spread of fire; 4. Ability to use and maintain various firefighting equipment; 5. Ability to temporarily prepare ropes, rope ladders, and safety nets; 6. Knowledge of fire rescue methods; 7. Knowledge of the structure and use of fire extinguishers; 8. Ability to assist the police in maintaining order during a fire alarm and to assist the fire brigade by passing buckets and guiding them to water sources; 9. Having participated in and practiced in five or more fire drills with certification.

(24) First Aid: 1. Ability to perform various methods of transporting injured persons; 2. Ability to make temporary stretchers and splints; 3. Knowledge of blood circulation and the location of major arteries; 4. Ability to perform hemostasis for internal and external bleeding; 5. Ability to provide first aid for fractures and dislocations; 6. Ability to provide emergency treatment for suffocation, burns, poisoning, wounds, spasms, fainting, and foreign objects in the eyes; 7. Ability to perform artificial respiration; 8. Ability to assemble a small, practical first aid kit.

(25) Rescue: 1. Ability to demonstrate four types of water rescue techniques and three types of escapes from a drowning person's grip; 2. Ability to use a lifeline or lifebuoy; 3. Ability to jump into water over two meters deep and retrieve objects; 4. Ability to perform artificial respiration and methods for increasing body temperature; 5. Ability to remove clothing and footwear in the water.

(26) Shooting: 1. Knowledge of shooting techniques with arrows, bows, air guns, pistols, rifles, etc.; 2. Ability to pass the marksmanship test using three of the following implements: A. Using arrows at a distance of six meters, achieving an average score of 50 or more out of five attempts; B. Using a bow at a distance of six meters, achieving an average score of 50 or more out of five attempts; C. Using an air gun at a distance of ten meters, achieving an average score of 50 or more out of five attempts; D. Using a pistol at a distance of ten meters, achieving an average score of 50 or more out of five attempts; E. Using a rifle at a distance of one hundred meters, achieving an average score of 50 or more out of five attempts. The standard target is defined as having a diameter of one meter, divided into twenty concentric red and white circles, with scores ranging from 5 for the outermost circle, increasing by 5 for each circle inward, up to 100 for the center; 3. Knowledge of the care and maintenance of bows, arrows, and firearms.

Joint University of Shanghai's Sorrowful Appeal to the Soldiers of the 19th Route Army: Pointing Guns Inward is Self-Estrangement from the People 丨Also Encouraging all Shanghai Students to Sharpen Their Resolve to Quell the Rebellion 198

The Joint Student Union of Shanghai Universities yesterday issued a sorrowful appeal to the soldiers of the 19th Route Army and a letter of encouragement to all Shanghai students. These are recorded separately below.

Appeal to the 19th Route Army 199

To all the soldiers of the 19th Route Army in Fuzhou: In these days of internal and external troubles, when the survival of the nation is on the line, uniting for rescue is still precarious. Yet, we have heard that Chen Mingshu, Li Jishen, and others have usurped Fuzhou, falsely using the name of our 19th Route Army to rally rebellious parties, advocating alignment with the communists, seceding from the party, changing the national flag, and spreading alarming messages. These actions by Chen Mingshu and his cohorts are driven by ulterior motives, aiming to rebel against the party and disrupt the nation. Their ultimate disgrace is not worth pitying. However, our 19th Route Army, with its glorious history, is now being held hostage by a few, incurring a disgraceful name. This would not only be a significant loss to the national spirit but also bring joy to our enemies while causing grief to those who support us. Alas, the white bones of the revolutionary martyrs of the Northern Expedition have not yet cooled, and the blood of the soldiers who died in the fight against the Japanese and in the suppression of the communists is still fresh. Our loyal and brave soldiers of the 19th Route Army, who earned their reputation by resisting the Japanese, suppressing the communists, and not participating in internal wars, are now pointing their guns inward, willingly becoming the leaders of those who destroy the party and the nation. This is no less than self-estrangement from the people and a destruction of their own history. If the martyrs who resisted the Japanese and suppressed the communists were aware of this, they would weep bitterly in their graves. We deeply believe that many soldiers in the 19th Route Army understand righteousness. Their enthusiasm for cherishing their own precious history and their conscience for safeguarding the survival of the nation and the people may be temporarily obscured by the deception of treacherous individuals, but eventually, they will deeply reflect and strive to extricate themselves. During the January 28 Incident in Shanghai, we, the students of all universities in Shanghai, were fortunate to have some association with your army, either through offering supplies or sharing the battlefield. We dare to express our humble opinions and tearfully appeal to you. We hope that you will awaken to the truth, put righteousness above family, arrest all the treacherous villains and offer them to the central government, and abolish the illegal organization to apologize to the people. This is the only way to preserve the glorious reputation of the 19th Route Army and save the nation from its imminent demise. The decision rests on this moment. We would be most fortunate if you would heed our words. Respectfully, the Joint Student Union of Shanghai Universities.

Letter of Encouragement to all Shanghai Students 200

The national crisis is more severe than ever. To overcome this difficult situation, we must unite and strengthen our defenses, be mindful of the dangers of a collapsing nest and broken eggs, and prepare for a desperate last stand. Yet, news has arrived that Chen Mingshu and others have colluded with the communists, forming a puppet government in Fujian and carrying out a rebellion. This heartbreaking and insane behavior is self-estrangement from the people and will soon collapse. It is not a major threat. However, our union still feels compelled to address all university students in Shanghai. This time, the Fujian Incident, in its abandonment of the national title and its changing of the flag, is a clear demonstration of being a puppet of the Soviet Union, a fact that is universally recognized. Its slogans of dividing farmers, workers, merchants, scholars, and soldiers further indicate its integration with the communists in Jiangxi. Under these circumstances, suppressing the rebellion is suppressing the communists, and suppressing the communists is suppressing the rebellion. Quelling the rebellion and suppressing the communists are now one and the same. Therefore, we should strengthen our resolve, rise up, and, under the leadership of the central government, bravely move forward, remaining calm and fighting hard, without complacency or fear of difficulty. We must ensure that all 50,000 university students in Shanghai become the backbone of suppressing the rebellion and stabilizing the country, eliminating the source of this internal turmoil, striving for the survival of the nation, and seeking a way out for the people. Our union is willing to encourage all students in Shanghai to work together. Respectfully, the Joint Student Union of Shanghai Universities.

Sports, The Last Five Minutes: Jiaotong Defeats Fudan, One to Zero丨Zhou Guangzhong Scores at the Last Moment丨Both Sides Attack and Defend Vigorously 201

In the Jiangnan University Football Championship, there was an important match yesterday, Jiaotong versus Fudan, meeting in Xujiahui to compete for the final spot. This is because Jinan University is assured of a final spot, and besides Jiaotong and Fudan, no one else is capable of challenging Jinan for the final. Yesterday, the Jiaotong University football field was surrounded by spectators. The two teams were evenly matched, and amidst the roaring cheers, they fought fiercely for 85 minutes without a breakthrough. Finally, in the last five minutes, Jiaotong's Zhou Guangzhong scored a goal, deciding the outcome. The referee was Shen Huichun.

One Attack, One Defense 202

Jiaotong excels at attacking, while Fudan excels at defending, creating yesterday's situation. Jiaotong's five forwards coordinated well, and the midfield also provided support. Shen Guanlan was a strong center back. Thus, Jiaotong was frequently seen circling around Fudan's goal, but Fudan's defense was strong, with Yang Mingquan's goalkeeping being particularly outstanding, along with the defenders Guan Xun'an and Zhang Rong. Therefore, yesterday's match was a contest between attack and defense. It's a pity that Jiaotong's forwards lacked finishing ability, otherwise, Jiaotong would have won earlier.

Zero to Zero 203

The entire first half of 45 minutes was dominated by Jiaotong, which relentlessly attacked Fudan. Chen Gongyu made a good pass, and Wan Xianghua received it and sprinted forward, but the center forward lacked strength and missed the opportunity. Then, the right winger Xue Wenxiu made a brilliant pass, and Tong Guangzhong jumped up to head the ball, but Yang Mingquan also jumped up and lightly tapped the ball, which fell to the left wing, creating a very dangerous situation. Wan Xianghua rushed up but failed to get the ball. These were some of the highlights of the first half. With one attack and one defense, the first half ended zero to zero.

The Last Kick 204

In the second half, each side made one or two substitutions. Fudan showed signs of resurgence and launched fierce counterattacks. Wang Wenjing made two forward rushes on the left wing with great momentum. Yu Shunzhang once tried to head the ball but failed. Zhou Shaowen and others gave their all, but gradually showed signs of fatigue. Jiaotong's counterattacks returned. Wan Xianghua made three attempts on goal, but all failed. A draw seemed inevitable. Unexpectedly, in the last five minutes, Xue Wenxiu dribbled up the left wing and crossed the ball. Without warning, Zhou Guangzhong had already flashed in front of the goal and lightly tapped the ball in. Guan Xun'an was caught off guard. This one kick sealed the victory.

Jinan Defeats Jinling丨Three to Zero丨 205

(Nanjing, 25th) In the Jiangnan University Football Championship, Jinan played against Jinling at 3:00 PM on the 25th at the Jinan University stadium. The referee was Zhang Xinfu. After the kickoff, Jinan attacked fiercely, repeatedly advancing towards Jinling. After forty minutes, Xu Yahui kicked in a goal, making the score one to zero in the first half. After the start of the second half, Jinan's attack was even more intense. Within four minutes, Jinan's Fu Hexuan scored another goal. At this point, Jinling's situation was dire. Although they wanted to counterattack, they were unable to do so because Jinan's attack and defense were both excellent. Finally, Xu Yahui scored another goal, making the score two to zero in the second half. As a result, Jinan defeated Jinling by a score of three to zero.

Central Defeats Great China丨Two to One丨 206

(Nanjing, 25th) In the Jiangnan University Football Championship, Central played against Great China at 2:30 PM on the 25th at the Central University stadium. The referee was Wang Jing. Within the first fifteen minutes of the match, Lin Ding, Central University's cross-country star, passed the ball to Wu Shunwen, who casually took a hard and powerful shot directly at Great China's goal. The goalkeeper could not defend it, resulting in a goal. Seeing their poor formation, the Great China team launched a fierce attack for a long time. After resting, within the first five minutes, the ball reached Central University's goal. Goalkeeper Jiang Lianggui had already caught the ball, but accidentally slipped and fell, causing the ball to fall from his hands. Huang Guanzhi arrived just in time and kicked it in, effortlessly. The first half ended in a one-to-one tie. After the break, the teams switched sides and resumed play. Central University's attack was even more intense, and the ball was often in front of Great China's goal. Great China was under attack and on the verge of collapse, so they adjusted their strategy and adopted a defensive stance. Central University had many good shots, but they were all blocked by the goalkeeper. With three minutes remaining, Central University launched a fierce forward attack. Li Pan kicked the ball forcefully, hitting the top crossbar of Great China's goal, and it swirled down. Xu Yusu used his body to block the goalkeeper, preventing him from using his catching skills, so the ball fell into the goal, resulting in a score of one to zero in the second half. As a result, Central University defeated Great China by a score of two to one.

Scott Cup: Yau Yau Eliminated Yesterday丨Rangers Wins Four to Three丨Yau Yau Led Twice 210

Rangers played Yau Yau yesterday. The forwards and defenders on both sides were worth watching. Although Yau Yau was ahead with a score of two to one in the first half, they were constantly under intense pressure from the opponent, and the situation was unfavorable. Not long after the start of the second half, Rangers' center back took a long shot, forcing a tie. After that, Yau Yau took the lead again with a score of three to two, but Rangers soon caught up and won with a score of four to three. Some spectators, acting emotionally, expressed various dissatisfactions with Yau Yau. This is not only inappropriate but also lacks the proper attitude of a spectator.

Stealing the Golden Needle 211

Yau Yau kicked off, but Rangers intercepted the ball halfway and launched a major counterattack, repeatedly forcing corner kicks. As a result, the area in front of Yau Yau's goal was full of danger. Fortunately, Wang Shusen repeatedly saved the day. However, because Rangers' forwards continued to attack relentlessly, Huang Ruihua headed out a ball, which was obtained by Simons, who passed it to Alger nearby. With trouble on the western front and the central hub shaken, Haberk stole the golden needle from Wang Shusen. Rot saw the joy of Rangers, pulled back a ball and passed into the gate.

Two Goals in Return 212

After Rangers scored a goal, their momentum became even stronger. Tang Yongchun was very busy, punching and kicking. Within ten minutes, they barely managed to hold on. Sun Tie-leg furiously commanded his troops and launched a counterattack. A-Qiao was slippery and unpredictable, and he quickly entered the defense, picking out a central hub. Sun Tie-leg dribbled the ball, and Li Shuoyou wanted to shoot but couldn't and fell. However, Li Shuoyou received help from Xi Qiaosheng. Inside the penalty area, Sun Jinshun fought with Chin Sheng. Little Li found an opportunity to shoot, resulting in a tie. After ten minutes of melee, Chen Jiaqiu passed to Xi Qiaosheng. A-Qiao passed it to Zhong Nansen, hesitated a little, and the ball went to Tie-leg, who dribbled it into the gate, making it two to one, turning defeat into victory.

Taking the Lead Again 213

After the break, with the applause and cheers of the Western spectators, Rangers made progress. The momentum of their attack was very grand. Huang Ruihua sent the ball out of danger twice, but still couldn't protect the territory. Simons broke into the Yau Yau's central defense line at seven minutes, took advantage of people's unpreparedness, and shot hard, Tang Yongchun was caught off guard, and it became a tie again. Alger had been selected for the inter-port team, and his skill was unquestionable. Twice he passed urgent balls to Yau Yau's gate, Rot headed the ball twice but missed, which annoyed Sun Jinshun, who launched a northern expedition, rushing forward alone like a downpour. The two defenders, Chin and Locke, were no match and were unable to resist, and Cochran lost his mind, leaving the old nest, so Sun scored into the empty gate, making it three to two.

Ultimately Failing 214

After Yau Yau took the lead again, their momentum could not be sustained. After several back-and-forths, Rangers launched a fierce counterattack. Haberk watched Sun Jinshun, Simons blocked Li Shiyou, and Alger roamed around the east, entering the area guarded by Zhuang Shihong, and passed to Haberk. Outside Yau Yau's goal line, they entangled for a while. Baosailie kicked the ball, Tang Yongchun's vision was blocked by the two defenders, and by the time he glimpsed the ball, it was too late to save it, and he slid into the net from the edge. Not long after, Simons again had the opportunity to fire a shot from thirty yards, creating a four-three situation. After this, Sun Jinshun had two urgent shots, but unfortunately they were slightly off target. He was eliminated in the Scott Cup with a score of three to four.

Middle School Cross-Country Race Next Month on the 22nd at Daxia Affiliated Middle School, Registration Deadline is the 15th of Next Month 221

The Cross-Country Race Committee of the Shanghai Middle School Sports Federation held a meeting at the Sports Promotion Association the day before yesterday. The attendees were Xu Zheng (Chairman), Huang Huaiying, Huang Quan, and three others. The minutes of the meeting are listed below:

(1) Date: December 22nd (Friday) at 2:30 PM. Those who arrive more than 20 minutes late will be considered to have forfeited.

(2) Location: Daxia University Affiliated Middle School, Fanhuangdu Zhongshan Road.

(3) Route: Starting from the entrance of Daxia University, heading north along Zhongshan Road, directly to the Zhabei Water and Electricity Plant. The round trip should not exceed 5,000 meters at most, and at least 4,500 meters. The detailed route will be drawn by Daxia Affiliated Middle School and distributed to each school.

(4) Registration: From now until 6:00 PM on December 15th. Registration location: Xu Zheng, Sports Department, Pudong Middle School, Liuli Bridge, Pudong.

(5) Number of participants: Each school can register a maximum of 10 people and a minimum of 6 people. The list of names must be submitted at the time of registration.

(6) Scoring: Sequential scoring method will be used, i.e., the first place gets 1 point, the second place gets 2 points, and so on. The official score for each school will be based on the first six people to reach the finish line.

(7) Championship: The team with the lowest total score of the first six people to reach the finish line will win the championship. The scoring method will be calculated using the reverse scoring method.

(8) Referees: Will be hired by the committee.

(9) Marshals: Will be undertaken by the Boy Scout Troupe of Daxia Affiliated Middle School.

The Autumn Colors of Jiangnan are About to Fade: Wangping Street Football Team Established: Assembling the Elite of the "Old Men's Army": If Anyone Dares to Provoke, They Will Surely Face the Consequences 223

Although the west wind is strong, it cannot blow away the autumn scenery of the Huangpu River. The chrysanthemums are plump, still retaining the autumn colors of Jiangnan. Plus, the weather is neither cold nor hot, making it the perfect time for athletes to show their skills. Therefore, we have decided to, in addition to our usual work of cutting and pasting, also engage in the game of football. Representative Assembly of the China Table Tennis Federation 228

The Shanghai China Table Tennis Federation held a representative assembly of each team at the Postal Workers' Club last night (23rd) to re-elect officials and organize the second Federation Cup competition. A total of 24 member teams attended, including Guangdong, Postal Team A, Jiande, Hongzhang, and Lingnan. Former President Wu reported the purpose of the meeting, followed by a speech by former Secretary-General Xu Duo, who also reported on the previous session's work. Then, former Accountant Yang Xiqing reported on the previous session's income and expenditure accounts. All representatives then amended the constitution, changing the previous president system to a committee system. It was officially decided to have nine executive committee members, three alternate members, three supervisory committee members, and one alternate member. The first executive and supervisory committee members were then elected by ballot. As a result, Xu Duo, Hu Jiankun, Liu Keren, Chen Zhensheng, Lu Zhongqiu, Kang Jiwen, Cao Zhendong, Wu Jiangleng, and Liu Guoxiong were elected as executive committee members. Cheng Linsheng, Cheng Zhihong, and Gao Yucheng were elected as alternate executive committee members. Xu Duo, Hu Jiankun, Liu Keren, Kang Jiwen, and Wu Jiangleng were nominated as standing committee members, and Lu Xiulu was nominated as standing supervisor. Finally, the matters concerning this year's cup competition were discussed. It was decided to continue using the single round-robin system without grouping. The competition will use Zero Two standard balls produced by the China Table Tennis Company, which will be provided by the association. The venues will be temporarily located at Postal Team A, Lund, Guangdong Hongzhang, Fenjiao, and Puguang Lingnan, where they will be held separately. The opening date will be decided by the executive committee and then notified in writing to facilitate the competition. The meeting then adjourned.
